  70 | _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE = threading.local()
  71 | 
  72 | 
  73 | @contextmanager
  74 | def single_equation_evaluation():
  75 |     """
  76 |     Enforce the benchmark contract for one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call.
  77 | 
  78 |     A candidate may build helper subexpressions, but it may submit exactly one
  79 |     symbolic template to the scorer. This prevents reward hacking where a
  80 |     program tries many equations and returns whichever receives the best score.
  81 |     """
  82 |     previous = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
  83 |     state = _SingleEquationState()
  84 |     _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = state
  85 |     try:
  86 |         yield
  87 |         if state.calls != 1:
  88 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
  89 |                 "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must call "
  90 |                 "evaluate_expression() exactly once with one symbolic equation template. "
  91 |                 f"It submitted {state.calls} templates. Build one base equation and let "
  92 |                 "the harness fit that equation's constants per dataset."
  93 |             )
  94 |     finally:
  95 |         _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = previous
  96 | 
  97 | 
  98 | def _record_scored_template(template: sp.Expr) -> None:
  99 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 100 |     if state is None:
 101 |         return
 102 | 
 103 |     state.calls += 1
 104 |     fingerprint = sp.srepr(template)
 105 |     if state.template_fingerprint is None:
 106 |         state.template_fingerprint = fingerprint
 107 |         return
 108 | 
 109 |     if state.template_fingerprint != fingerprint:
 110 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 111 |             "Single-equation violation: one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call "
 112 |             "submitted multiple different symbolic equation templates. The base "
 113 |             "equation must be fixed; only fitted constants may change."
 114 |         )
 115 | 
 116 |     raise SingleEquationViolation(
 117 |         "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() called "
 118 |         "evaluate_expression()/fit_expression_constants() more than once. Do not "
 119 |         "try multiple equation templates or multiple scorer calls and pick the "
 120 |         "best result; submit exactly one symbolic expression."
 121 |     )

 125 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 126 |     if state is not None:
 127 |         state.result_snapshot = copy.deepcopy(result)
 128 |

 130 | def validate_single_equation_result(result: Any) -> None:
 131 |     """
 132 |     Ensure the candidate returns the actual scorer output, unchanged.
 133 | 
 134 |     This closes the loophole where a program calls evaluate_expression() once
 135 |     to satisfy the call-count guard, then fabricates or edits the metrics it
 136 |     returns to the evaluator.
 137 |     """
 138 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 139 |     if state is None:
 140 |         return
 141 | 
 142 |     if state.result_snapshot is None:
 143 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 144 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "

 149 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(

  24 |     GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS,
  25 |     GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS,
  26 | )
  27 | 
  28 | 
  29 | class SingleEquationViolation(RuntimeError):
  30 |     """Raised when a candidate tries to score more than one equation template."""
  31 | 
  32 | 
  33 | MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY = int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY", "160"))
  34 | MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS = int(os.environ.get("SKYDISCOVER_MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS", "12"))
  35 | _BANNED_EXPR_TYPES = (
  36 |     sp.Piecewise,
  37 |     Relational,
  38 |     BooleanFunction,
  39 |     sp.Heaviside,
  40 |     sp.DiracDelta,
  41 | )
  42 | _BANNED_EXPR_FUNCTIONS = {
  43 |     "Max",
  44 |     "Min",
  45 |     "sign",
  46 |     "floor",
  47 |     "ceiling",
  48 |     "Mod",
  49 | }
  50 | 
  51 | 
  52 | @dataclass(frozen=True)
  53 | class FittedExpression:
  54 |     """A fitted symbolic expression and its validation predictions."""
  55 | 
  56 |     expression_template: sp.Expr
  57 |     expression: sp.Expr
  58 |     constants: dict[str, float]
  59 |     y_pred_train: NDArray
  60 |     y_pred_val: NDArray
  61 | 
  62 | 
  63 | @dataclass
  64 | class _SingleEquationState:
  65 |     calls: int = 0
  66 |     template_fingerprint: str | None = None
  67 |     result_snapshot: dict[str, Any] | None = None
  68 | 
  69 | 
  70 | _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE = threading.local()
  71 | 
  72 | 
  73 | @contextmanager
  74 | def single_equation_evaluation():
  75 |     """
  76 |     Enforce the benchmark contract for one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call.
  77 | 
  78 |     A candidate may build helper subexpressions, but it may submit exactly one
  79 |     symbolic template to the scorer. This prevents reward hacking where a
  80 |     program tries many equations and returns whichever receives the best score.
  81 |     """
  82 |     previous = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
  83 |     state = _SingleEquationState()
  84 |     _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = state
  85 |     try:
  86 |         yield
  87 |         if state.calls != 1:
  88 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
  89 |                 "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must call "
  90 |                 "evaluate_expression() exactly once with one symbolic equation template. "
  91 |                 f"It submitted {state.calls} templates. Build one base equation and let "
  92 |                 "the harness fit that equation's constants per dataset."
  93 |             )
  94 |     finally:
  95 |         _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = previous
  96 | 
  97 | 
  98 | def _record_scored_template(template: sp.Expr) -> None:
  99 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 100 |     if state is None:
 101 |         return
 102 | 
 103 |     state.calls += 1
 104 |     fingerprint = sp.srepr(template)
 105 |     if state.template_fingerprint is None:
 106 |         state.template_fingerprint = fingerprint
 107 |         return
 108 | 
 109 |     if state.template_fingerprint != fingerprint:
 110 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 111 |             "Single-equation violation: one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call "
 112 |             "submitted multiple different symbolic equation templates. The base "
 113 |             "equation must be fixed; only fitted constants may change."
 114 |         )
 115 | 
 116 |     raise SingleEquationViolation(
 117 |         "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() called "
 118 |         "evaluate_expression()/fit_expression_constants() more than once. Do not "
 119 |         "try multiple equation templates or multiple scorer calls and pick the "
 120 |         "best result; submit exactly one symbolic expression."
 121 |     )
 122 | 
 123 | 
 124 | def _record_scorer_result(result: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 125 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 126 |     if state is not None:
 127 |         state.result_snapshot = copy.deepcopy(result)
 128 | 
 129 | 
 130 | def validate_single_equation_result(result: Any) -> None:
 131 |     """
 132 |     Ensure the candidate returns the actual scorer output, unchanged.
 133 | 
 134 |     This closes the loophole where a program calls evaluate_expression() once
 135 |     to satisfy the call-count guard, then fabricates or edits the metrics it
 136 |     returns to the evaluator.
 137 |     """
 138 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 139 |     if state is None:
 140 |         return
 141 | 
 142 |     if state.result_snapshot is None:
 143 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 144 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 145 |             "the dictionary produced by evaluate_expression()."
 146 |         )
 147 | 
 148 |     if result != state.result_snapshot:
 149 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 150 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 151 |             "the exact, unmodified result from its single evaluate_expression() "
 152 |             "call. Do not fabricate, overwrite, wrap, or post-process metrics."
 153 |         )
 154 | 
 155 | 
 156 | def feature_symbols(n_features: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
 157 |     """Create PySR-compatible feature symbols x0, x1, ..."""
 158 |     return create_sympy_symbols([f"x{i}" for i in range(n_features)])
 159 | 
 160 | 
 161 | def constant_symbols(n_constants: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
 162 |     """Create tunable constant symbols c0, c1, ..."""
 163 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]
 164 | 
 165 | 
 166 | def pysr_operator_names() -> dict[str, list[str]]:
 167 |     """Return the PySR operator vocabulary exposed to evolved equation builders."""
 168 |     return {
 169 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 170 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 171 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 172 |     }
 173 | 
 174 | 
 175 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
 176 |     """
 177 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
 178 | 
 179 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
 180 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
 181 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
 182 |     """
 183 |     return {
 184 |         **sympy_mappings,
 185 |         "pi": sp.pi,
 186 |         "E": sp.E,
 187 |     }
 188 | 
 189 | 
 190 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
 191 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
 192 |         return expression
 193 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))
 194 | 
 195 | 
 196 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
 197 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
 198 | 
 199 | 
 200 | def _validate_expression_template(template: sp.Expr, constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol]) -> None:
 201 |     complexity = int(_complexity(template))
 202 |     if complexity > MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY:
 203 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 204 |             "Single-equation violation: symbolic template is too complex "
 205 |             f"({complexity} nodes > limit {MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY}). Do not hide "
 206 |             "many candidate equations inside one oversized expression."
 207 |         )
 208 | 
 209 |     if len(constants) > MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS:
 210 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 211 |             "Single-equation violation: too many fitted constants "
 212 |             f"({len(constants)} > limit {MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS}). Use one compact "
 213 |             "universal equation, not an over-parameterized surrogate."
 214 |         )
 215 | 
 216 |     for node in sp.preorder_traversal(template):
 217 |         if isinstance(node, _BANNED_EXPR_TYPES) or node.func.__name__ in _BANNED_EXPR_FUNCTIONS:
 218 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
 219 |                 "Single-equation violation: conditional, piecewise, discontinuous, "
 220 |                 f"or gated symbolic construct '{node.func.__name__}' is not allowed. "
 221 |                 "Use one smooth global equation template."
 222 |             )
 223 | 
 224 | 
 225 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
 226 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
 227 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
 228 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 229 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
 230 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
 231 |         else:
 232 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
 233 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 234 | 
 235 | 
 236 | def fit_expression_constants(
 237 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 238 |     X_train: NDArray,
 239 |     y_train: NDArray,
 240 |     X_val: NDArray,
 241 |     *,
 242 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 243 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 244 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 245 | ) -> FittedExpression:
 246 |     """
 247 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 248 | 
 249 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 250 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 251 |     """
 252 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 253 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 254 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 255 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 256 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 257 |     _record_scored_template(template)
 258 | 
 259 |     if constants is None:
 260 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 261 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 262 |     constants = list(constants)
 263 |     _validate_expression_template(template, constants)
 264 | 
 265 |     if not constants:
 266 |         return FittedExpression(
 267 |             expression_template=template,
 268 |             expression=template,
 269 |             constants={},
 270 |             y_pred_train=_predict(template, X_train, feature_names),
 271 |             y_pred_val=_predict(template, X_val, feature_names),
 272 |         )
 273 | 
 274 |     if initial_values is None:
 275 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 276 |     else:
 277 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 278 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 279 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 280 | 
 281 |     feature_syms = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
 282 |     X_cols = [X_train[:, i] for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 283 | 
 284 |     # Compile expression once upfront so the residual avoids repeated
 285 |     # SymPy subs() + sympy2numpy() calls (the main bottleneck).
 286 |     try:
 287 |         _compiled = sp.lambdify(feature_syms + constants, template, modules=["numpy"])
 288 |         _test_args = X_cols + [float(v) for v in x0]
 289 |         _test_out = np.asarray(_compiled(*_test_args), dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 290 |         if _test_out.shape != y_train.shape:
 291 |             raise ValueError("shape mismatch")
 292 |         _use_compiled = True
 293 |     except Exception:
 294 |         _use_compiled = False
 295 | 
 296 |     if _use_compiled:
 297 |         def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 298 |             try:
 299 |                 args = X_cols + [float(v) for v in theta]
 300 |                 prediction = np.asarray(_compiled(*args), dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 301 |             except Exception:
 302 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 303 |             if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 304 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 305 |             return prediction - y_train
 306 |     else:
 307 |         def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 308 |             substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 309 |             candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 310 |             try:
 311 |                 prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 312 |             except Exception:
 313 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 314 |             if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 315 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 316 |             return prediction - y_train
 317 | 
 318 |     import warnings
 319 | 
 320 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 321 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 322 |         result = least_squares(
 323 |             residual,
 324 |             x0,
 325 |             loss="soft_l1",
 326 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 327 |         )
 328 |     fitted_constants = {
 329 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 330 |     }
 331 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 332 |     fitted_expr = template.subs(substitutions)
 333 | 
 334 |     return FittedExpression(
 335 |         expression_template=template,
 336 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 337 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 338 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 339 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 340 |     )
 341 | 
 342 | 
 343 | def evaluate_expression(
 344 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 345 |     X_train: NDArray,
 346 |     y_train: NDArray,
 347 |     X_val: NDArray,
 348 |     y_val: NDArray,
 349 |     *,
 350 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 351 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 352 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 353 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 354 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 355 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 356 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 357 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 358 |         expression,
 359 |         X_train,
 360 |         y_train,
 361 |         X_val,
 362 |         constants=constants,
 363 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 364 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 365 |     )
 366 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 367 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 368 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 369 | 
 370 |     result = {
 371 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 372 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 373 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 374 |         "loss": loss,
 375 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),
 376 |         "nmse_train": nmse_train,
 377 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 378 |         "combined_score": combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val),
 379 |     }
 380 |     _record_scorer_result(result)
 381 |     return result

  63 | @dataclass
  64 | class _SingleEquationState:
  65 |     calls: int = 0
  66 |     template_fingerprint: str | None = None
  67 |     result_snapshot: dict[str, Any] | None = None

  69 | 
  70 | _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE = threading.local()
  71 | 
  72 | 
  73 | @contextmanager
  74 | def single_equation_evaluation():
  75 |     """
  76 |     Enforce the benchmark contract for one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call.
  77 | 
  78 |     A candidate may build helper subexpressions, but it may submit exactly one
  79 |     symbolic template to the scorer. This prevents reward hacking where a
  80 |     program tries many equations and returns whichever receives the best score.
  81 |     """
  82 |     previous = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
  83 |     state = _SingleEquationState()
  84 |     _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = state
  85 |     try:
  86 |         yield
  87 |         if state.calls != 1:
  88 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
  89 |                 "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must call "
  90 |                 "evaluate_expression() exactly once with one symbolic equation template. "
  91 |                 f"It submitted {state.calls} templates. Build one base equation and let "
  92 |                 "the harness fit that equation's constants per dataset."
  93 |             )
  94 |     finally:
  95 |         _SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE.state = previous
  96 | 
  97 | 
  98 | def _record_scored_template(template: sp.Expr) -> None:
  99 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 100 |     if state is None:
 101 |         return
 102 | 
 103 |     state.calls += 1
 104 |     fingerprint = sp.srepr(template)
 105 |     if state.template_fingerprint is None:
 106 |         state.template_fingerprint = fingerprint
 107 |         return
 108 | 
 109 |     if state.template_fingerprint != fingerprint:
 110 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 111 |             "Single-equation violation: one evaluate_symbolic_candidate() call "
 112 |             "submitted multiple different symbolic equation templates. The base "
 113 |             "equation must be fixed; only fitted constants may change."
 114 |         )
 115 | 
 116 |     raise SingleEquationViolation(
 117 |         "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() called "
 118 |         "evaluate_expression()/fit_expression_constants() more than once. Do not "
 119 |         "try multiple equation templates or multiple scorer calls and pick the "
 120 |         "best result; submit exactly one symbolic expression."
 121 |     )
 122 | 
 123 | 
 124 | def _record_scorer_result(result: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
 125 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 126 |     if state is not None:
 127 |         state.result_snapshot = copy.deepcopy(result)
 128 | 
 129 | 
 130 | def validate_single_equation_result(result: Any) -> None:
 131 |     """
 132 |     Ensure the candidate returns the actual scorer output, unchanged.
 133 | 
 134 |     This closes the loophole where a program calls evaluate_expression() once
 135 |     to satisfy the call-count guard, then fabricates or edits the metrics it
 136 |     returns to the evaluator.
 137 |     """
 138 |     state = getattr(_SINGLE_EQUATION_STATE, "state", None)
 139 |     if state is None:
 140 |         return
 141 | 
 142 |     if state.result_snapshot is None:
 143 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 144 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 145 |             "the dictionary produced by evaluate_expression()."
 146 |         )
 147 | 
 148 |     if result != state.result_snapshot:
 149 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 150 |             "Single-equation violation: evaluate_symbolic_candidate() must return "
 151 |             "the exact, unmodified result from its single evaluate_expression() "
 152 |             "call. Do not fabricate, overwrite, wrap, or post-process metrics."
 153 |         )

 156 | def feature_symbols(n_features: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
 157 |     """Create PySR-compatible feature symbols x0, x1, ..."""
 158 |     return create_sympy_symbols([f"x{i}" for i in range(n_features)])
 159 | 
 160 | 
 161 | def constant_symbols(n_constants: int) -> list[sp.Symbol]:
 162 |     """Create tunable constant symbols c0, c1, ..."""
 163 |     return [sp.Symbol(f"c{i}", real=True) for i in range(n_constants)]

 166 | def pysr_operator_names() -> dict[str, list[str]]:
 167 |     """Return the PySR operator vocabulary exposed to evolved equation builders."""
 168 |     return {
 169 |         "unary": GENERAL_UNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 170 |         "binary": GENERAL_BINARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 171 |         "ternary": GENERAL_TERNARY_OPERATORS.copy(),
 172 |     }

 175 | def pysr_operator_namespace() -> dict[str, Any]:
 176 |     """
 177 |     Return PySR-to-SymPy operator callables usable in expression templates.
 178 | 
 179 |     Operators like ``+``, ``-``, ``*``, and ``/`` should be written with normal
 180 |     Python syntax. Named PySR operators such as ``sin``, ``cos``, ``sqrt``,
 181 |     ``log1p``, ``max``, ``min``, ``muladd``, and ``clamp`` are exposed here.
 182 |     """
 183 |     return {
 184 |         **sympy_mappings,
 185 |         "pi": sp.pi,
 186 |         "E": sp.E,
 187 |     }

 190 | def _as_sympy_expr(expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> sp.Expr:
 191 |     if isinstance(expression, sp.Expr):
 192 |         return expression
 193 |     return pysr2sympy(expression, feature_names_in=list(feature_names))

 195 | 
 196 | def _complexity(expression: sp.Expr) -> float:
 197 |     return float(sum(1 for _ in sp.preorder_traversal(expression)))
 198 | 
 199 | 
 200 | def _validate_expression_template(template: sp.Expr, constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol]) -> None:
 201 |     complexity = int(_complexity(template))
 202 |     if complexity > MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY:
 203 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 204 |             "Single-equation violation: symbolic template is too complex "
 205 |             f"({complexity} nodes > limit {MAX_EQUATION_COMPLEXITY}). Do not hide "
 206 |             "many candidate equations inside one oversized expression."
 207 |         )
 208 | 
 209 |     if len(constants) > MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS:
 210 |         raise SingleEquationViolation(
 211 |             "Single-equation violation: too many fitted constants "
 212 |             f"({len(constants)} > limit {MAX_EQUATION_CONSTANTS}). Use one compact "
 213 |             "universal equation, not an over-parameterized surrogate."
 214 |         )
 215 | 
 216 |     for node in sp.preorder_traversal(template):
 217 |         if isinstance(node, _BANNED_EXPR_TYPES) or node.func.__name__ in _BANNED_EXPR_FUNCTIONS:
 218 |             raise SingleEquationViolation(
 219 |                 "Single-equation violation: conditional, piecewise, discontinuous, "
 220 |                 f"or gated symbolic construct '{node.func.__name__}' is not allowed. "
 221 |                 "Use one smooth global equation template."
 222 |             )
 223 | 
 224 | 
 225 | def _predict(expression: sp.Expr, X: NDArray, feature_names: Sequence[str]) -> NDArray:
 226 |     symbols = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
 227 |     fn = sympy2numpy(expression, symbols)
 228 |     with np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 229 |         if isinstance(fn, CallableEquation):
 230 |             y_pred = fn(np.asarray(X, dtype=float))
 231 |         else:
 232 |             y_pred = fn(*[X[:, i] for i in range(X.shape[1])])
 233 |     return np.asarray(y_pred, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 234 | 
 235 | 
 236 | def fit_expression_constants(
 237 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 238 |     X_train: NDArray,
 239 |     y_train: NDArray,
 240 |     X_val: NDArray,
 241 |     *,
 242 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 243 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 244 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 245 | ) -> FittedExpression:
 246 |     """
 247 |     Fit free constants in a SkyDiscover-proposed expression template.
 248 | 
 249 |     The expression structure is supplied by the evolved program. This helper only
 250 |     performs the continuous inner fit and PySR-style export/evaluation.
 251 |     """
 252 |     X_train = np.asarray(X_train, dtype=float)
 253 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 254 |     X_val = np.asarray(X_val, dtype=float)
 255 |     feature_names = [f"x{i}" for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 256 |     template = _as_sympy_expr(expression, feature_names)
 257 |     _record_scored_template(template)
 258 | 
 259 |     if constants is None:
 260 |         feature_set = set(feature_symbols(X_train.shape[1]))
 261 |         constants = sorted(template.free_symbols - feature_set, key=lambda s: s.name)
 262 |     constants = list(constants)
 263 |     _validate_expression_template(template, constants)
 264 | 
 265 |     if not constants:
 266 |         return FittedExpression(
 267 |             expression_template=template,
 268 |             expression=template,
 269 |             constants={},
 270 |             y_pred_train=_predict(template, X_train, feature_names),
 271 |             y_pred_val=_predict(template, X_val, feature_names),
 272 |         )
 273 | 
 274 |     if initial_values is None:
 275 |         x0 = np.ones(len(constants), dtype=float)
 276 |     else:
 277 |         x0 = np.asarray(initial_values, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 278 |         if x0.size != len(constants):
 279 |             raise ValueError("initial_values must match the number of constants")
 280 | 
 281 |     feature_syms = create_sympy_symbols(feature_names)
 282 |     X_cols = [X_train[:, i] for i in range(X_train.shape[1])]
 283 | 
 284 |     # Compile expression once upfront so the residual avoids repeated
 285 |     # SymPy subs() + sympy2numpy() calls (the main bottleneck).
 286 |     try:
 287 |         _compiled = sp.lambdify(feature_syms + constants, template, modules=["numpy"])
 288 |         _test_args = X_cols + [float(v) for v in x0]
 289 |         _test_out = np.asarray(_compiled(*_test_args), dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 290 |         if _test_out.shape != y_train.shape:
 291 |             raise ValueError("shape mismatch")
 292 |         _use_compiled = True
 293 |     except Exception:
 294 |         _use_compiled = False
 295 | 
 296 |     if _use_compiled:
 297 |         def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 298 |             try:
 299 |                 args = X_cols + [float(v) for v in theta]
 300 |                 prediction = np.asarray(_compiled(*args), dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 301 |             except Exception:
 302 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 303 |             if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 304 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 305 |             return prediction - y_train
 306 |     else:
 307 |         def residual(theta: NDArray) -> NDArray:
 308 |             substitutions = {symbol: float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, theta)}
 309 |             candidate = template.subs(substitutions)
 310 |             try:
 311 |                 prediction = _predict(candidate, X_train, feature_names)
 312 |             except Exception:
 313 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 314 |             if prediction.shape != y_train.shape or not np.all(np.isfinite(prediction)):
 315 |                 return np.full_like(y_train, 1e12, dtype=float)
 316 |             return prediction - y_train
 317 | 
 318 |     import warnings
 319 | 
 320 |     with warnings.catch_warnings(), np.errstate(over="ignore", divide="ignore", invalid="ignore"):
 321 |         warnings.simplefilter("ignore", RuntimeWarning)
 322 |         result = least_squares(
 323 |             residual,
 324 |             x0,
 325 |             loss="soft_l1",
 326 |             max_nfev=max_nfev,
 327 |         )
 328 |     fitted_constants = {
 329 |         str(symbol): float(value) for symbol, value in zip(constants, result.x)
 330 |     }
 331 |     substitutions = dict(zip(constants, result.x))
 332 |     fitted_expr = template.subs(substitutions)
 333 | 
 334 |     return FittedExpression(
 335 |         expression_template=template,
 336 |         expression=fitted_expr,
 337 |         constants=fitted_constants,
 338 |         y_pred_train=_predict(fitted_expr, X_train, feature_names),
 339 |         y_pred_val=_predict(fitted_expr, X_val, feature_names),
 340 |     )
 341 | 
 342 | 
 343 | def evaluate_expression(
 344 |     expression: sp.Expr | str | float | int,
 345 |     X_train: NDArray,
 346 |     y_train: NDArray,
 347 |     X_val: NDArray,
 348 |     y_val: NDArray,
 349 |     *,
 350 |     constants: Sequence[sp.Symbol] | None = None,
 351 |     initial_values: Sequence[float] | None = None,
 352 |     max_nfev: int = 300,
 353 | ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 354 |     """Score a proposed equation template after fitting its constants."""
 355 |     y_train = np.asarray(y_train, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 356 |     y_val = np.asarray(y_val, dtype=float).reshape(-1)
 357 |     fitted = fit_expression_constants(
 358 |         expression,
 359 |         X_train,
 360 |         y_train,
 361 |         X_val,
 362 |         constants=constants,
 363 |         initial_values=initial_values,
 364 |         max_nfev=max_nfev,
 365 |     )
 366 |     nmse_train = nmse(y_train, fitted.y_pred_train)
 367 |     nmse_val = nmse(y_val, fitted.y_pred_val)
 368 |     loss = float(np.mean((fitted.y_pred_train - y_train) ** 2))
 369 | 
 370 |     result = {
 371 |         "equation_template": str(fitted.expression_template),
 372 |         "equation": str(fitted.expression),
 373 |         "constants": fitted.constants,
 374 |         "loss": loss,
 375 |         "complexity": _complexity(fitted.expression_template),
 376 |         "nmse_train": nmse_train,
 377 |         "nmse_val": nmse_val,
 378 |         "combined_score": combined_score_from_nmse(nmse_val),
 379 |     }
 380 |     _record_scorer_result(result)
 381 |     return result
